One thing that I can say about Rubio's and probably not many people know is that they have real keto friendly options this being the keto shells they use with any Taco you want.

The Keto shell is basically a grilled cheese Circle that is used as a tortilla and it's really crunchy and adds lots of flavor to the different fish or shrimp proteins available.< /Review>

< Review>
Louise is an artist, and I come every Friday (for years) to get my drink. You wont find your perfect coffee at Starbucks or Dutch, but you can find it here. The little homemade cakes are to die for, surprisingly filling, and I'm not ashamed to say I've walked out with a half dozen or more before. You simply wont get that kind of taste and quality out of the big name's frozen and freeze dried, long distance shipped, pastries.

I drove past this gem for years before I stopped in. Don't make that mistake too. Skip Starbucks one morning and get the coffee you deserve.< /Review>

<Time>1549076338032< /Time><rating>5< /rating><text>What can I say, I've been coming here for almost 20 years. It's a great family owned restaurant where you actually have husband and wife working almost every day with their sons. They truly monitor there quality of food and you will receive the same dish that you've had before. One thing I always come back here for and crave are the egg rolls. They do a great job not using too much egg roll wrapper. If you don't know what I mean, picture biting into an eggroll where you feel like your teeth are trying to cut through five layers of the wrapper just to get to the filling. You won't find this at Pho Bo Vang. The egg rolls have a wonderful texture and flavor and are totally addictive. I love all of their different types of pho and rice vermicelli noodles.

If you don't know what to order ask Tommy or Toby. They'll recommend something good for you!</text>< Pics>

< Review>
I have tried most of the Pho places south of Irvine and they don't compare to Pho Bo Vang.
Their pho is pretty phenomenal with a great price point and a generous serving of meat and noodles. Their broth is delicious and doesn't have the aftertaste of sugar trying to hide lack of quality. No no, they do not cut corners here and serve delicious soup.
Heavily recommend the wonton soup(so fresh), all stir fry recipes(never knew stir fry could taste so GOOD), and their fried rice combinations.
Don't look no further,  this isn't just a pho shop,  its Vietnamese cuisine done right.</Review>

<name>Jason Lum<//name>< time>
1458229645076< /time>
< Text>
I'm not Vietnamese, but for any crazy pho lover the pho must be exceptional. Secondly, Who goes to a place that has Pho in the name to order fried rice? EatPho people! PhoOOoo-Shizzle! Before you think I'm a harsh critic take the time to my review...

I am a loyal Thanh Binh II fan. Not because it's better than every place in Westminster, but it is THE BEST PHO IN LAKE FOREST. I attempted to try something difference and see what all the fuse is about.  Pho Bo Vang was getting great reviews. Why not?

When I first drove up to this restaurant you better know what you are looking for. It's located in a shady questionable strip mall. Not a ideal place near a thrift store and other rundown businesses. Although, tutto famiglia next store looks bomb. I could really go for some homemade hole-in-the-wall Italian. The parking lot was packed. I was thinking wow! There was actually a wait outside (restaurant is pretty small though). And you have to sign up on a small paper list, kind of like when you go to small sushi restaurants. All good signs so far. I saw Asian people another plus and require to authorize any Asian cuisine. Cough* PF Chang. Cough* BS!

Here goes nothing.. Here's the Throwdown of Thanh Binh II  vs. Pho Bo Vang! Yeah it's on. Nobody Pho-k Up! It's going down and somebody's getting Served!

PRO (Pho Bo Vang wins)
-CLEAN! This is an understatement. VERY VERY VERY CLEAN! Tables are clean and don't look old. Very fashionable high end Asian/Japanese type table setting and dinningware. (This doesn't effect the taste nor does it matter. This is Pho not a fine Filet Minon.)
-Nice presentation. The condiments and side veggies are very clean and crisp. The hot sauce looks like a new bottle and not like refilled bottle from 10 years ago. Even the meat in my Pho was lined up neatly similar to like bowl of Japanese Ramen. HMMm. I wish I had Ramen.
-Service is friendly and quick to clean tables, but smelling ozone killing chemicals while trying to eat in a small restaurant, BAD IDEA! Soup and water would be fine.
-The rare beef steak is RARE!!! That itself is rare a lot of pho places give you well done even when you clearly ordered RARE!
-Meat is good quality but lacking on quantity.

CONS (Thanh Binh II wins)
-A bit pricey for Pho, which is traditional cheap.
-THE KILLER!!! I was ready to give PBV a 4 or more rating, but the one thing that matters most in Pho. Not the meat, not the amount of noodles, and not the hot sauce... THE SOUP!!! The soup should taste like it took 48 hours to make and came out of a small kitchen in Vietnam. The soup should look like a meaty broth. PBV looked like water and chicken both. At least throw some MSG in there, because this soup lacked flavor!!!! I was in disbelief. I tried to add more condiments and plum sauce to make the soup look the part. EPIC FAIL.
-You call this Extra-Large? PSSHH! You charge me 9 bucks and I could eat another meal after this. Sadly, I accidentally ate a small meal before, but polished this INSULT off easily. TB2 wins by a landslide, normal people 2 or 1 me can finish their Super Bowl.
-Ordered Egg Rolls and PBV looked like Chinese egg rolls. Viet egg rolls taste a little different and sometimes have more meat and you can usually wrap it in fresh veggies. PBV CHARGES FOR extra wrap lettuce! It says a BUCK MORE on the menu itself. Are SERIOUS???! When was lettuce not free with the egg rolls? PBV you can take that cucumber and SHOVE IT!

Conclusions. I don't think I will ever go back, but if I do I'm actually going to skip on the Pho and just order a rice plate. That's against my Pho rule, but if you make soup like PBV.... At least, use can Pho broth like other places. Approved for non-Asians. Cleaniness tends to attract more customers because of an A Health rating not for the food. It's about the food people. Wake up.</Text>

< text>
This is the freshest "fast food" I've ever eaten. I actually thought I didn't like falafel until I tried it here. Usually its dry and hard.. not here! Everything at Vanoos is made fresh.. in other words it is NOT prepared from a package! They start with the actual garbanzo bean! Omg you can tell. The best part was.. I didn't even order that! The owner offered it after I raved about the gyro she prepared.  The owner must have noticed how much I appreciate food cooked with love.. you can tell she puts all her attention and intent on crafting a fine meal and delivering it hot and fresh. The dolmas, again - incredibly fresh. All the reviews are true people!

A word about the gyro - the content was like everything I describe above - fresh and high quality. Other things to appreciate are the proportions and cut of the food in the gyro. Everything was sliced thin so that all the ingredients could layer and you could taste everything in a bite. Imagine a gyro where each piece of vegetable and meat is cut in chunks so you basically have to choose one ingredient per bite.. this happened SOMEWHERE else.. so thank you Vanoos Grillette for doing it right! I really enjoyed my meal and your warm welcome!</text>

< text>
My husband and I used to love this place. This last time we bought the chicken dinner. On a scale from 1-10, it was a 5.
We also bought 4 different cakes/cheesecake. They looked good but were absolutely horrible!
I could not believe that they sold us the cakes/cheesecakes as they were old and tasted like they had been in the refrigerator for quite a while. I was upwraping these, I noticed the date they were sliced and packaged on the styrofoam plate and the date was 5 days prior. And who knows how long it was made before then! As you may or may not know, these old deserts are not cheap. I spent over $20 for just 4 of them. If they were fresh, they might have been worth it.
I WOULD NEVER RECOMMEND BUYING ANY OF THEIR DESERTS TO ANYONE. And the chicken dinner ($28) was mediocre at best. The 4 broasted potatoes had black spots in them so we had to throw those away as well. The best part of this purchase of over $52 was the coleslaw. That is alot of money just to enjoy coleslaw!<//text>

The deli has moved from their old Eastland Center location to 126 E Shoppers Ln, in Covina just a couple of blocks north. The restaurant space is better but finding a parking space can be a challenge during peak hours. <Rate>1</Rate><Review>I have been going here for years. Joe the owner got me hooked on their Lox & Cream cheese on Sourdough bread. My husband & I go often because we like to give business to local business.
When I order the Lox& Cream cheese on sourdough I always pay for extra lox without hesitation.

Tonight we went in at 4:30  to get take out. It was the second time I have ordered this to go and paid extra and when I opened the bag at home I did not get extra lox that I paid for. I live in Walnut which is too far to go back so they can correct their mistakes!

Please bring another Old World closer to the Inland Empire!<//Review>
<Pics>None<//Pics><response>None< /response><gmap_id>0x80c3285294ce9a57:0x58464adc56972ad7< /gmap_id></record>

0x80c3285294ce9a57:0x58464adc56972ad7</Gmap_id>
< Text>
WHAT IT IS
A FULL Italian deli. They stock BOARS HEAD MEATS (!!!), so there's a source of them in West Covina! Get the Everroast Chicken--your taste buds will love you. In addition to the meats, they have various salads and the ubiquitous Italian cookies.

They also have a restaurant section where they serve "Broasted" chicken, sandwiches, pizza, and soups. Please note--it's tucked away on Shopper's Lane, so it can be a little hard to find if you aren't used to the area.

WHAT YOU SHOULD ORDER
Sandwiches, deli meat

AMBIANCE
5 stars
I really like the look of this place. When you enter, you're standing in the deli portion of the store (which is partitioned from the dining room by a shelf). They have the full line of Boar's Head products including their flavored mayonnaise and mustard. The deli counter is to your right--the bar to order food is directly ahead. There's also a little dessert case right next to where you order your food to tempt you.

The dining room is nice and open and features a salad bar--a rarity in this day and age. This location is relatively new and it shows--everything is clean and lovely looking.

FOOD AND DRINKS
5 Stars
I am in love with their chicken salad sandwich. I've never had a chicken salad so good--I usually don't like chicken salad because I hate celery--but they ground everything up so finely that it comes out more like a delicious spread than a chunky salad. They serve that sandwich on a kaiser roll complete with poppy seeds, which just makes the east coaster in me super happy. I've never tried the chicken, but it smells quite good. I've also not tried the pizza.

NICE SURPRISES
Fruit tarts! One of my favorite little dainty desserts, and yet it's so hard to find outside of the Mexican super markets. And they're good, too!

OVERALL
A fantastic little deli for West Covina!<//Text>
